<sup>1</sup>H       1.007825  99.985%   1/2  +2.79284
<sup>2</sup>H       2.0140    0.015%    1    +0.85743
</pre><b>Notes:</b><br><br> 
 The wavelengths and energy levels given below are for the isotope <sup>1</sup>H.                   
<BR><BR>                                                                                            
 Although the tabulated energy levels comprise values for each level through n = 5,                 
 we give (Ritz) wavelengths for resolved fine structures only for the Lyman-alpha,                  
 Balmer-alpha, and Balmer-beta lines (1215, 6562, and 4861 &#197;).  As indicated by the            
 energy-level notations in the persistent-lines table, the other wavelengths represent              
 unresolved multiplets.  These wavelengths are from the corresponding weighted-average              
 energies.                                                                                          
<BR><BR>                                                                                            
<pre> 
H I  Ground State 1<i>s</i>  <Sup>2</sup>S<sub>1</sub><sub>/</sub><sub>2</sub>
